<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прочный.html>про́чный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">próčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прочность.html>про́чность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">próčnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прочность.html>про́чности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прочность.html>про́чности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прочность.html>про́чностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>durability, solidity, firmness, strength, fastness

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прочность.html>про́чность</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:изгиб.html>изги́б</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>próčnostʹ</b> na izgíb</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">bending strength</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запас.html>запа́с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прочность.html>про́чности</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zapás <b>próčnosti</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">safety factor; safety margin</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испытывать.html>испы́тывать</a> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прочность.html>про́чность</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ispýtyvatʹ štó-libo na <b>próčnostʹ</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">test the durability of smth</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испытывать.html>испы́тывать</a> кого́-л <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прочность.html>про́чность</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ispýtyvatʹ kovó-l na <b>próčnostʹ</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">put smb to the test; test smb's patience</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***прочтение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прочтение.html>прочте́ние</a> (15926)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">прочт-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pročt-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прочтение.html>прочте́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pročténije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прочтение.html>прочте́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прочтение.html>прочте́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прочтение.html>прочте́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>reading, perusal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прочтение.html>прочте́нии</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po <b>pročténii</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">on reading;after perusal</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>reading, interpretation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прочтение.html>прочте́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:симфония.html>симфо́нии</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nóvoje <b>pročténije</b> simfónii</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">a new reading of the symphony</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:прочь.html>прочь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pročĭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">away</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">проче</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proče</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">except</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">пріч</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">precz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span Per Vasmer, apparently an original comparative of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*prokъ</i> (whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прок.html>прок</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), originally an adjective meaning "ahead". See <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прочее.html>про́чий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">próčij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прок.html>прок</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for more information.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прочь.html>прочь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pročʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>away, aside</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прочь.html>прочь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pročʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>be off, get out</li>
<li>begone, away with you</li>
<li>beat it, <a href = vnd.unilang:скат.html>scat</a></li>
<li>hence</li></ol>

***прошествие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прошествие.html>проше́ствие</a> (16734)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прошествие.html>проше́ствие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prošéstvije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прошествие.html>проше́ствия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прошествие.html>проше́ствия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прошествие.html>проше́ствий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>in expressions only</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прошествие.html>проше́ствии</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po prošéstvii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">after the lapse; after the expiration</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прошествие.html>проше́ствии</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пяти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po <b>prošéstvii</b> pjatí let</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">after five years had elapsed; five years later</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>шить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прошить.html>проши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prošítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прошива́ть</b>)

***прошлый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прошлый.html>про́шлый</a> (269)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прошлый.html>про́шлый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">próšlyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>last, past
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прошлый.html>про́шлой</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ле</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>próšloj</b> nedéle</i> ― <span class="e-translation">last week</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прошлый.html>про́шлом</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>году́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>próšlom</b> godú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">last year</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>former</li></ol>

</p>

***прощать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прощать.html>проща́ть</a> (2449)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простить.html>прости́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощать.html>проща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простить.html>прости́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to forgive, to pardon, to excuse</li>
<li>to remit</li>
<li>to condone, to overlook</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperative  only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to farewell</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освобождать.html>освобожда́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">osvoboždátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ща́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:простить.html>прости́ть</a>.
<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́нии</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:извинить.html>извини́ть</a>»: <a href = vnd.unilang:прощать.html>проща́ть</a> <i>кому-то что-то</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:либо.html>ли́бо</a> <i>кого-то <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> что|то</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́нии</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:освобождать.html>освобожда́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долгий.html>долга</a>»: <a href = vnd.unilang:прощать.html>проща́ть</a> <i>кому|то что|то</i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-прощ-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ща́<span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ю<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>щий</b>
